           The `basemotion` facts include `basemotion(#q9, #o0, #o3)` and `basemotion(#o3, #o0, #q0)`. This implies that `#o3` *is* a base configuration that the robot can move to and from. The problem then must be in what `btraj` values are actually allowed. My usage of `#o0` was likely incorrect for transitions.
           
           Let's strictly use the provided `move_base` actions.
           
           1.  **Move v8 (from v9, to p5):**
               *   To pick: `atbconf(#q9)`. Path from `v3`: `(move_base v3 #q9 #t22)`. This is explicitly listed as a valid action.

               *   To place: `atbconf(#o3)`. Path from `#q9` to `#o3`?
                   *   Searching for `(move_base #q9 #o3 <btraj>)` in the allowed list: *None found*.
                   *   This is the core of the problem. `#o3` is used in `kin` for `place` but no `move_base` action exists to get to `#o3`.
           
           This suggests that either:
           a) `#o3` is not meant to be a base configuration that the robot moves to directly, but rather is a placeholder for the robot being "in the vicinity" for that specific kinematic action.
           b) There's an indirect path via other `q`s that I need to find.
           c) The problem is unsolvable as stated due to conflicting information (i.e., `place` actions requiring `#o3` but no way to get there).
           
           Given that I MUST provide a valid plan, option c) is not acceptable. Option a) seems most plausible given the `kin` predicates. Perhaps the `kin` actions with `#o3` imply the base config is automatically handled. However, previous errors state `atbconf` preconditions are not met.
